    SELECT [d].[DEPT_ID], [d].[COST_CENTER_CODE], [d].[DEPT_NAME_AR], [d].[DEPT_NAME_EN], [d].[IS_ACTIVE], [d].[MANAGER_ID], [d].[PARENT_DEPT_ID]

    WHERE [d].[IS_DELETED] = CAST(0 AS tinyint)
    ORDER BY [d].[DEPT_NAME_AR]

) AS [d1]
